Earlier this year we highlighted A Child\u2019s Place, Make A Wish, Special Olympics, and Rollin\u2019 Hornets.  After a year of Covid and virtual learning, we wanted to partner with a nonprofit that\u2019s helping to educate our youth in Charlotte. We were connected with Augustine Literacy Project who provides tutors to kids who have fallen behind in reading, writing, and spelling.  ALP focuses on kids who are at least one year behind in reading and come from a low income family with free and reduced lunches.  I was shocked to hear that kids only have a 1 in 8 chance of catching up if they fall behind in reading by 1st grade!  Like A Child is donating $15,000 to Augustine Literacy Project that will allow them to expand and provide tutors to an entire new school here in Charlotte! Rise and Read!!!
